      <h2 class="screen-reader-text">
       Main navigation
      </h2>
      <nav aria-label="Main navigation" class="nav-primary" id="genesis-nav-primary" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/SiteNavigationElement">
       <div class="menu-a-main-menu-container">
        <ul class="genesis-nav-menu" id="menu-a-main-menu">
         <li class="menu-item menu-item-type-post_type menu-item-object-page menu-item-6484621 half-half" id="menu-item-6484621">
          <a href="https://www.gsu.edu/about/" title="About Georgia State University">
           About

     function revslider_showDoubleJqueryError(sliderID) {
					var errorMessage = "Revolution Slider Error: You have some jquery.js library include that comes after the revolution files js include.";
					errorMessage += "<br> This includes make eliminates the revolution slider libraries, and make it not work.";
					errorMessage += "<br><br> To fix it you can:<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 1. In the Slider Settings -> Troubleshooting set option:  <strong><b>Put JS Includes To Body</b></strong> option to true.";
					errorMessage += "<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 2. Find the double jquery.js include and remove it.";
					errorMessage = "<span style='font-size:16px;color:#BC0C06;'>" + errorMessage + "</span>";
						jQuery(sliderID).show().html(errorMessage);
				}
    </script>

var blendModes = ['normal', 'multiply', 'screen', 'overlay', 'darken', 'lighten', 'color-dodge', 'color-burn', 'hard-light', 'soft-light', 'difference', 'exclusion', 'hue', 'saturation', 'color', 'luminosity'];
 
if('CSS' in window && 'supports' in window.CSS) {
 
    jQuery('.rev_slider li[data-mediafilter]').each(function() {
 
        for(var i = 0; i < blendModes.length; i++) {
 
            if(!window.CSS.supports('mix-blend-mode', blendModes[i])) {
 
                this.removeAttribute('data-mediafilter');
                break;
 
            }
 
        }
 
    });
